   function readCookie(name)
        {
            var nameEQ = name + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
            }
            return null;
        }
        
        function load_wt_dcstracking(parameter, value)
        {
            if(typeof dcsMultiTrack == 'undefined')
            {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    load_wt_dcstracking(parameter, value);
                }, 1000)
            }
            else
            {
                dcsMultiTrack('WT.dl', '99', parameter, value );
            }
        }

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function getParameterByName(name)
    {
        name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\\]");
        var regexS = "[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)";
        var regex = new RegExp(regexS,'i');
        var results = regex.exec(window.location.search);
        if(results == null)
            return "";
        else
            return decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
    }
	function checkWebTrendsMetaTag(){
            if (typeof $ !== "undefined") {
                var srch	= $('meta[name=WT\\.srch]');
		var webTrendsMetaTagExists = false;
		if( srch.length > 0 && $(srch).attr('content') == '1'){
			webTrendsMetaTagExists = true;
		}
		return webTrendsMetaTagExists;
        }
        else {
            setTimeout(checkWebTrendsMetaTag, 50);
        }
    }
    function is_GA_required()
    {
        //Show GA by default
        var output = true;

        //If we have decided earlier to supress GA, then continue to do so
        if (readCookie("show_GA") != null && readCookie("show_GA") == "false")
        {
            output = false;
        }
        else if (readCookie("show_GA") == null) //If no cookie is present
        {
            var qs_src  = getParameterByName('WT.qs_src');
            var srch    = getParameterByName('WT.srch');
			var webTrendsMetaTagExists = checkWebTrendsMetaTag();
            if (qs_src != "" || (srch != "" && srch == 1) || webTrendsMetaTagExists == true)
            {
                //Cookie that will expire at end of session
                document.cookie = "show_GA=false; path=/";
                output = false;
            }
        }
        return output;
    }
    var GA_required = is_GA_required();
  </script>

   if (GA_required == true)

   String.prototype.endsWith = function (suffix) {
    return this.indexOf(suffix, this.length - suffix.length) !== -1;
};

var jquery_wait_count = 0;

function Attach_jQuery() {
    var fileref = document.createElement("script");
    fileref.setAttribute("type", "text/javascript");
    fileref.setAttribute("src", "//ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/1.7.2/jquery.min.js");
    var parent = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];
    parent.insertBefore(fileref, parent.childNodes[0]);
}

function check_for_jquery() {
    //call self jquery not found
    var function_name = 'check_for_jquery';
    //For Lampdev time is set for 15sec and Stage time is set for 25 sec and for prod max time will be 5 sec, please take care while integrating 
    if (jquery_wait_count == 5) {
        //call attach_jquery if jquery not found after 10 counts
        function_name = 'Attach_jQuery'
    }
    if (typeof jQuery == "undefined") {
        jquery_wait_count += 1;
        setTimeout(function_name + '()', 1000);
    }
}

var AutoNewModel = {
    new_tab_window : '',
    getZipErrorMessage: function (zipcode_type)
    {
        var ca_error_msg = 'Please enter a valid Canada postal code.';
        var us_error_msg = 'Please enter a valid US zip code.';
        var error_msg = 'Please enter a valid US or Canada postal code.';
        if (zipcode_type == 'US')
        {
            return us_error_msg;
        }
        else if (zipcode_type == 'Canada')
        {
            return ca_error_msg;
        }
        else
        {
            return error_msg;
        }
    },
    showFormErrors: function (error, form)
    {
        var newmodel = this;
        newmodel.clearAllFormErrors(form);
        if (error[0].field == 'form')
        {
            newmodel.addErrorFlag(form, error[0].message);
        }
        else
        {
            for (x in error)
            {
                var location = '';
                if (error[x].field == 'zip' || error[x].field == 'insured')
                {
                    location = form + ' input[name="' + error[x].field + '"]';
                    var select_remove_outline = form + ' div[id="user_carrier_container"]';
                    $(location).addClass('formError');
                    $(select_remove_outline).removeClass('formError');
                    newmodel.addErrorFlag(location, error[x].message);
                    return false;
                }
                /* IQW select option validation issue  for insurance.com auto insurance state pages */
                else if (error[x].field == 'user_carrier')
                {
                    location = form + ' div[id="' + "user_carrier_container" + '"]';
                    var input_remove_outline = form + " input[name='zip']";
                    $(location).addClass('formError');
                    $(input_remove_outline).removeClass('formError');
                    location = form + ' select[name="' + error[x].field + '"]';
                    newmodel.addErrorFlag(location, error[x].message);
                    return false;
                }
                else
                {
                    newmodel.clearAllFormErrors(form);
                    location = form;
                    newmodel.clearInputError(form);
                }
            }
        }
    },
    trimWhiteSpaces: function (str)
    {
        return (str != '' && str != null && typeof str === 'string')
                ? str.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '')
                : '';
    },
    clearAllFormErrors: function (form)
    {
        jQuery(form).find('.errorFlag').remove('.errorFlag');
        jQuery(form).find("div:visible[id*='error_msg']").hide();
    },
    clearInputError: function (location)
    {
        jQuery(location).siblings('.errorFlag').remove();
        jQuery(location).removeClass('formError');
    },
    addErrorFlag: function (location, message)
    {
        var newmodel = this;
        var field = $(location).parent('fieldset');

        /* IQW select option validation issue  for insurance.com auto insurance state pages */
        if (location.match(/select/))
        {
            var field = $(location).parent('div');
            jQuery(field).prepend('<div class="errorFlag" style="right:-12px; top:-91px;"><div class="paddingWrapper"><a href="void()" class="close">x</a><p>' + message + '</p></div></div>');
            jQuery(location).siblings('.errorFlag').children('.paddingWrapper').children('.close').click(function (j) {
                j.preventDefault();
                newmodel.clearInputError(location);
            });
            return false;
        }
        if (jQuery(field).children('[id^=' + $(location).attr('name') + '_error_msg]').length > 0)
        {
            jQuery(field).children('[id^=' + $(location).attr('name') + '_error_msg]').show();
        }
        else
        {
            jQuery(field).prepend('<div class="errorFlag"><div class="paddingWrapper"><a href="void()" class="close">x</a><p>' + message + '</p></div></div>');
            jQuery(location).siblings('.errorFlag').children('.paddingWrapper').children('.close').click(function (j) {
                j.preventDefault();
                newmodel.clearInputError(location);
            });
        }
    },
    sendAlert: function (xhr_request, xhr_status, post_data, quote_loc)
    {
        var debug_data = '';
        var newmodel = this;

        quote_loc = quote_loc.replace('#', '');

        if (typeof (post_data) == 'string')
        {
            debug_data = post_data;
        }
        else
        {
            if (post_data.state != 'undefined' && post_data.state != null)
            {
                debug_data += '&state=' + post_data.state;
            }
            if (post_data.zip != 'undefined' && post_data.zip != null)
            {
                debug_data += '&zip=' + post_data.zip;
            }
            if (post_data.insured != 'undefined' && post_data.insured != null)
            {
                debug_data += '&insured=' + post_data.insured;
            }
        }

        jQuery.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '//' + document.domain + '/autonewmodel/emailalert',
            data: 'where=' + quote_loc +
                    '&action=' + encodeURIComponent($('#' + quote_loc).attr('action')) +
                    '&product=LB auto' +
                    '&errorDescription=' + newmodel.trimWhiteSpaces(xhr_request) +
                    '&ajxStatus=' + xhr_status +
                    debug_data
        });
    },
    isValidUSZip: function (zip)
    {
        return /^[0-9]{5}(?:-[0-9]{4})?$/.test(zip);
    },
    isValidState: function (state)
    {
        return /^[A-Za-z]{2}$/.test(state);
    },
    isValidCanadaZip: function (zip)
    {
        return /^[ABCEGHJKLMNPRSTVXY][0-9][A-Z][\s]?[0-9][A-Z][0-9]$/.test(zip);
    },
    getUniqueValues: function (arrayName)
    {
        var newArray = new Array();

        label:for (var i = 0; i < arrayName.length; i++)
        {
            for (var j = 0; j < newArray.length; j++)
            {
                if (newArray[j] == arrayName[i])
                    continue label;
            }
            newArray[newArray.length] = arrayName[i];
        }
        return newArray;
    },
    formValidation: function (event, form)
    {
        var newmodel = this;
        var form_id = '#' + jQuery(form).attr('id');
        var data = window.location.search.substring(1) + '&' + jQuery(form).serialize();
        var data_arr = data.split('&');
        var unique_data_arr = this.getUniqueValues(data_arr);
        data = unique_data_arr.join('&');

        newmodel.clearAllFormErrors(form_id);
        newmodel.showFormErrors([{'field': 'form', 'message': 'Processing...'}], form_id);

        var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;

        if (/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(ua) && typeof Promise !== "undefined") {
            var promise_callback = new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
              jQuery.ajax({
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                url: jQuery(form).attr('action'),
                type: 'GET',
                data: data,
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function success(result) {
                    resolve(result);
                },
                error: function error(XHR, textStatus) {
                    var reject_obj = {
                        XHR_status: XHR,
                        text_status: textStatus
                    };
                    reject(reject_obj);
                }
              });
            });

            promise_callback.then(function(result) {
                if (result && result.errors.length == 0) {
                    if (result.newtab) {
                        AutoNewModel.new_tab_window = window.open('', 'newtab').focus();
                    }
                    newmodel.clearAllFormErrors(form_id);
                    newmodel.processFormRedirect(result);
                }
                else
                {
                    AutoNewModel.showFormErrors(result.errors, form_id);
                }
            }).catch(function(rejectObj){
                AutoNewModel.showFormErrors([{'field': 'form', 'message': 'An error has occured please try again.'}], form_id);
                newmodel.sendAlert(rejectObj.XHR_status, rejectObj.text_status, data, form_id);
            });
        } else {
            jQuery.ajax({
                async: false,
                cache: false,
                url: jQuery(form).attr('action'),
                type: 'GET',
                data: data,
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result && result.errors.length == 0)
                    {
                        newmodel.clearAllFormErrors(form_id);
                        newmodel.processFormRedirect(result);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        AutoNewModel.showFormErrors(result.errors, form_id);
                    }
                },
                error: function (XHR, textStatus) {
                    AutoNewModel.showFormErrors([{'field': 'form', 'message': 'An error has occured please try again.'}], form_id);
                    newmodel.sendAlert(XHR, textStatus, data, form_id);
                }
            });
        }
    },
    redirectQuote: function (event, refobj)
    {
        var newmodel = this;
        jQuery.ajax({
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            url: jQuery(refobj).attr('href'),
            type: 'GET',
            data: {},
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.errors.length == 0)
                {
                    newmodel.processFormRedirect(result);
                }
            },
            error: function (XHR, textStatus) {
                newmodel.sendAlert(XHR, textStatus, {}, 'In Article Link');
            }
        });
    },
    /*
     Redirection of NM lead form and lbrates page based on implementation type
     "leave_behind"        - opens NM lead form in PopUp and lbrates as leavebehind
     "nm_leave_behind"     - opens NM lead form as leave behind and lbrates in PopUp
     "quoteoptions_newtab" - opens NM lead form in new Tab and lbrates as leavebehind
     */
    processFormRedirect: function (data)
    {
        if (data.popup)
        {
            this.popupWindow(data.popup, 'newwindow');
        }
        if (data.newtab)
        {
            if(AutoNewModel.new_tab_window)
            {
                AutoNewModel.new_tab_window.location.href = window.location.origin + data.newtab;
                AutoNewModel.new_tab_window.focus();
            }
            else 
            {
                window.open(data.newtab, 'newtab');
            }
        }
        if (data.redirect)
        {
            this.redirectUrl(data.redirect);
        }
    },
    popupWindow: function (url, name)
    {
        var ua = jQuery.getBrowser();
        var x = (window.screenX || window.screenLeft || 0);
        var y = (window.screenY || window.screenTop || 0);
        var j = screen.width;
        var k = screen.height;
        if (ua.msie && ua.version.slice(0, 3) == '6.0')
        {
            window.open(url, name, "top=" + y + ", left=" + x + ", width=" + (j != null ? j : 1) + ",height=" + (k != null ? k : 1) + ",resizable=1,scrollbars=1,toolbar=1,menubar=1,location=1", false);
        }
        else
        {
            window.open(url, name, "top=" + y + ", left=" + x + ", width=" + (j != null ? j : 1) + ",height=" + (k != null ? k : 1) + ",resizable=1,scrollbars=1,toolbar=1,menubar=1,location=1", false).focus();
        }
    },
    redirectUrl: function (url)
    {
        var ua = jQuery.getBrowser();
        if (ua.msie && ua.version.slice(0, 3) == '6.0')
        {
            window.location.href(url);
        }
        else
        {
            window.location.href = url;
        }
    }
}

function autonewmodel_callback() {
    if (typeof jQuery !== "undefined")
    {
        jQuery.uaMatch = function (ua) {
            ua = ua.toLowerCase();
            var match = /(chrome)[ \/]([\w.]+)/.exec(ua) ||
                    /(webkit)[ \/]([\w.]+)/.exec(ua) ||
                    /(opera)(?:.*version|)[ \/]([\w.]+)/.exec(ua) ||
                    /(msie) ([\w.]+)/.exec(ua) ||
                    ua.indexOf("compatible") < 0 && /(mozilla)(?:.*? rv:([\w.]+)|)/.exec(ua) || [];
            return {
                browser: match[ 1 ] || "",
                version: match[ 2 ] || "0"
            };
        };

        jQuery.getBrowser = function () {
            if (!jQuery.browser) {
                var matched = jQuery.uaMatch(navigator.userAgent);
                var browser = {};
                if (matched.browser) {
                    browser[ matched.browser ] = true;
                    browser.version = matched.version;
                }
                // Chrome is Webkit, but Webkit is also Safari.
                if (browser.chrome) {
                    browser.webkit = true;
                } else if (browser.webkit) {
                    browser.safari = true;
                }
                jQuery.browser = browser;
            }
            return jQuery.browser;
        };

        jQuery(document).ready(function () {
            jQuery(document).on('click', 'a[href*="/autonewmodel/geo"], a[href*="/autonewmodel/state"], area[href*="/autonewmodel/state"]', function (e) {
                if (e.preventDefault) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                }

                AutoNewModel.redirectQuote(e, this);
            });

            jQuery(document).on('submit', 'form[action*="/autonewmodel/"]', function (e) {
                if (e.preventDefault) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                }

                /* Declare variables & set defaults */
                var zip_type = 'US'
                var zip_val = '';
                var zip_count = $(this).find('input[name="zip"]').length;
                var select_iqw = $(this).find('select[name="user_carrier"]').val();
                var insured_count = $(this).find('input[name="insured"]').length;
                var is_valid_zip = true; /* default true in case zip field is missing */
                var is_valid_insured = true; /* default true in case insured field is missing */
                var form_id = '#' + $(this).attr('id');

                /* Clear errors */
                AutoNewModel.clearAllFormErrors($(this).attr('id'));

                /* Validate zip */
                if (zip_count > 0)
                {
                    zip_val = $(this).find('input[name="zip"]').val();
                    if ($(this).attr('action').endsWith('/autonewmodel/ca'))
                    {
                        zip_type = 'Canada';
                        is_valid_zip = AutoNewModel.isValidCanadaZip(zip_val);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        if (AutoNewModel.isValidCanadaZip(zip_val))
                        {
                            zip_type = 'Canada';
                        }
                        else if (!AutoNewModel.isValidUSZip(zip_val))
                        {
                            is_valid_zip = false;
                        }
                    }
                }

                /* Validate insured */
                if (insured_count > 0)
                {
                    var input_type = $(this).find('input[name="insured"]').attr('type');
                    if (input_type == 'radio' && typeof $(this).find('input[name="insured"]:checked').val() == 'undefined')
                    {
                        is_valid_insured = false;
                    }
                }

                if (is_valid_zip === true && is_valid_insured === true)
                {
                    /* IQW select option validation issue  for insurance.com auto insurance state pages  */
                    if (select_iqw == "")
                    {
                        var error_arr = [{
                                'field': 'user_carrier',
                                'message': 'Please select your current insurer',
                            }];
                        var form_name = "#instant_quote_form";
                        AutoNewModel.showFormErrors(error_arr, form_name);
                        return false;
                    }
                    AutoNewModel.formValidation(e, this);
                }
                else if (!is_valid_zip)
                {
                    var error_arr = [{
                            'field': 'zip',
                            'message': AutoNewModel.getZipErrorMessage(zip_type)
                        }];
                    AutoNewModel.showFormErrors(error_arr, form_id);
                    return false;
                }
                else if (!is_valid_insured)
                {
                    var error_arr = [{
                            'field': 'insured',
                            'message': 'Answer must be selected.'
                        }];
                    AutoNewModel.showFormErrors(error_arr, form_id);
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });
    } else {
        setTimeout(autonewmodel_callback, 100);
    }
}

if (typeof jQuery == "undefined")
{
    check_for_jquery();
}
autonewmodel_callback();
  </script>
